RUS_setup_senate_duma_conflict_variables = {
	set_temp_variable = { bop_value = mp_support }
	divide_temp_variable = { bop_value = 550 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				var = bop_value
				value = 0.5
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			divide_temp_variable = { bop_value = -2 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		multiply_temp_variable = { bop_value = 2 }
	}
		
	set_power_balance = {
		id = RUS_senate_duma_conflict
		left_side = RUS_duma_side # will keep the last set side if not specified
		right_side = RUS_senate_side # will keep the last set side if not specified
		#set_default = yes # whether or not to reset the power balance to the initial value, default = no
		set_value = var:bop_value # if specified will set the value of the power balance, this option will override the effect of set_default so the two options should not be used together. if neither set_default or set_value is specified the current value of the power balance will not change
	}	
}
RUS_bop_low_increase_effect_10 = {
	add_power_balance_value = {
		id = RUS_senate_duma_conflict
		value = 0.10
	}
}

RUS_calculate_government_variables = {
	RUS_popular_support_recalc = yes
	RUS_army_support_recalc = yes
	RUS_average_support_recalc = yes
}
RUS_average_support_recalc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = popular_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = army_support }
	divide_temp_variable = { temp1 = 2 }
	set_variable = { average_pop_arm_support = temp1 }
}
RUS_popular_support_recalc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = party_popularity@ruling_party }
	set_temp_variable = { temp3 = 1 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp3 = modifier@consumer_goods_factor }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp3 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS.stability }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp2 < 0.5 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 0.5 }
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp2 = 1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { temp1 = additional_popular_support }
	set_variable = { popular_support = temp1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = popular_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
}
RUS_army_support_recalc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = party_popularity@ruling_party }
	set_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS.war_support }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { temp2 < 0.5 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp2 = 0.5 }
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp2 = 1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_dealt_with_army_mutiny }
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0.5 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { temp1 = additional_army_support }
	set_variable = { army_support = temp1 }
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = 1 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = army_support }
	set_variable = { opposite_army_support = temp1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = army_support
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
}
RUS_add_to_coalition = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist } 
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist } 
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = psr_coalition }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat } 
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { political_power_ideology = coalition_partner_var }
					is_in_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = add_to_coalition
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
					has_government = var:coalition_partner_var
					check_variable = { political_power_ideology = coalition_partner_var }
				}
			}
			add_to_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = party_popularity_dynamic_modifier_coalition }
					}
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = party_popularity_dynamic_modifier_coalition }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned } 
				}
				set_temp_variable = { psr_pp_gain = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
				divide_temp_variable = { psr_pp_gain = 2 }
				add_to_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = psr_pp_gain }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat } 
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { political_power_ideology = coalition_partner_var }
					is_in_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = add_to_coalition
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
					has_government = var:coalition_partner_var
					check_variable = { political_power_ideology = coalition_partner_var }
				}
			}
			add_to_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = party_popularity_dynamic_modifier_coalition }
					}
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = party_popularity_dynamic_modifier_coalition }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = psr_banned } 
				}
				set_temp_variable = { rsdrp_pp_gain = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
				divide_temp_variable = { rsdrp_pp_gain = 2 }
				add_to_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = rsdrp_pp_gain }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal } 
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal } 
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative } 
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat } 
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			OR = { 
				has_country_flag = national_populist_coalition
				has_country_flag = solidarist_coalition
			}
		}
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist } 
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}	
}
RUS_remove_from_coalition = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition
		clr_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist } 
		remove_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition
		clr_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist } 
		remove_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = psr_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = psr_coalition
		clr_country_flag = psr_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat } 
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_from_coalition
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = party_popularity_dynamic_modifier_coalition }
					check_variable = { coalition_partners^num = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition }
					set_temp_variable = { psr_pp_remove = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
					divide_temp_variable = { psr_pp_remove = 2 }
					subtract_from_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = psr_pp_remove }
				}
				else = {
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = party_popularity_dynamic_modifier_coalition }
					clear_variable = coalition_pp_gain
					clear_array = coalition_partners
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition }
					set_temp_variable = { psr_pp_remove = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
					divide_temp_variable = { psr_pp_remove = 2 }
					subtract_from_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = psr_pp_remove }
				}
				else = {
					remove_from_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
					subtract_from_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition_to_remove }
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat } 
		clr_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition
		clr_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition_to_remove
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_from_coalition
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = party_popularity_dynamic_modifier_coalition }
					check_variable = { coalition_partners^num = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = psr_coalition }
					set_temp_variable = { rsdrp_pp_remove = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
					divide_temp_variable = { rsdrp_pp_remove = 2 }
					subtract_from_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = rsdrp_pp_remove }
				}
				else = {
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = party_popularity_dynamic_modifier_coalition }
					clear_variable = coalition_pp_gain
					clear_array = coalition_partners
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = psr_coalition }
					set_temp_variable = { rsdrp_pp_remove = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
					divide_temp_variable = { rsdrp_pp_remove = 2 }
					subtract_from_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = rsdrp_pp_remove }
				}
				else = {
					remove_from_array = { coalition_partners = coalition_partner_var }
					subtract_from_variable = { coalition_pp_gain = party_popularity@var:coalition_partner_var }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition
		clr_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal } 
		remove_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition
		clr_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal } 
		remove_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition
		clr_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative } 
		remove_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition_to_remove }
		clr_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition
		clr_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition_to_remove
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat } 
		remove_from_coalition = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			OR = { 
				has_country_flag = national_populist_coalition_to_remove
				has_country_flag = solidarist_coalition_to_remove
			}
		}
		set_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist } 
		remove_from_coalition = yes
	}	
}

RUS_clear_all_coalitions = {
	clr_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition
	clr_country_flag = psr_coalition
	clr_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition
	clr_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition
	clr_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition
	clr_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition
	clr_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition
	clr_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition
	clr_country_flag = solidarist_coalition
	clr_country_flag = national_populist_coalition
	end_coalition = yes
}
RUS_setup_initial_senate = {
	set_variable = { plsr_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { plsr_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsp_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_total_senators = 1 }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators = 2 }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_presidential_senators = 2 }
	set_variable = { psr_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators = 17 }
	set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 6 }
	set_variable = { lkdp_total_senators = 1 }
	set_variable = { lkdp_total_regional_senators = 2 }
	set_variable = { lkdp_presidential_senators = 6 }
	set_variable = { rkdp_total_senators = 4 }
	set_variable = { rkdp_total_regional_senators = 1 }
	set_variable = { rkdp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { vns_total_senators = 37 }
	set_variable = { vns_total_regional_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { vns_presidential_senators = 20 }
	set_variable = { ep_total_senators = 5 }
	set_variable = { ep_total_regional_senators = 1 }
	set_variable = { ep_presidential_senators = 16 }
	set_variable = { nrpr_total_senators = 2 }
	set_variable = { nrpr_total_regional_senators = 5 }
	set_variable = { nrpr_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsnp_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsnp_total_regional_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsnp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { independent_total_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { independent_total_regional_senators = 22 }
	set_variable = { independent_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { senators_election_regional_total = 50 }
	set_variable = { senators_election_total = 50 }
	final_senators_recalc = yes
	calculate_half_senate = yes
	calculate_two_thirds_senate = yes
	calculate_half_duma = yes
	calculate_two_thirds_duma = yes
}
calculate_half_senate = {
	set_variable = { half_senate_plus_one = senate_total }
	divide_variable = { half_senate_plus_one = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { half_senate_plus_one = 1 }
	round_variable = half_senate_plus_one
}
calculate_two_thirds_senate = {
	set_variable = { two_thirds_senate_plus_one = senate_total }
	multiply_variable = { two_thirds_senate_plus_one = 2}
	divide_variable = { two_thirds_senate_plus_one = 3 }
	add_to_variable = { two_thirds_senate_plus_one = 1 }
	round_variable = two_thirds_senate_plus_one
}
calculate_half_duma = {
	set_variable = { half_duma_plus_one = mp_total }
	divide_variable = { half_duma_plus_one = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { half_duma_plus_one = 1 }
	round_variable = half_duma_plus_one
}
calculate_two_thirds_duma = {
	set_variable = { two_thirds_duma_plus_one = mp_total }
	multiply_variable = { two_thirds_duma_plus_one = 2}
	divide_variable = { two_thirds_duma_plus_one = 3 }
	add_to_variable = { two_thirds_duma_plus_one = 1 }
	round_variable = two_thirds_duma_plus_one
}

RUS_setup_initial_state_popularities = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_owned_by = RUS
					is_core_of = RUS
				}
				is_owned_by = TRM
				is_owned_by = FIN
				is_owned_by = ALO
				is_owned_by = UKR
				is_owned_by = WHR
				is_owned_by = KUB
				is_owned_by = DKB
				is_owned_by = KLY
				is_owned_by = GEO
				is_owned_by = ARM
				is_owned_by = POL
				is_owned_by = LIT
				is_owned_by = BAT
				is_owned_by = GAL
				is_owned_by = ROM
				is_owned_by = MTR
				is_owned_by = AZE
				is_owned_by = KYR
				is_owned_by = TRK
				is_owned_by = UZB
				is_owned_by = MON
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS.RUS_party_pop_states_array = THIS }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_general_turnout = 0.7 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_senate_turnout = 0.3 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout = 0.2 }
		set_variable = { RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout = 1 }
		#RUS_clamp_all_state_pop = yes
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 215
				state = 216
				state = 401
				state = 236
				state = 1197
				state = 1199
				state = 256
				state = 1193
				state = 399
				state = 397
				state = 651
				state = 1194
				state = 880
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS.RUS_minority_states = THIS }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 215
				state = 216
				state = 401
				state = 236
				state = 1197
				state = 1199
				state = 256
				state = 1193
				state = 399
				state = 397
				state = 651
				state = 1194
				state = 880
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS.RUS_minority_states = THIS }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_siberia = yes
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS.RUS_siberian_states = THIS }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 265
				state = 239
				state = 250
				state = 401
				state = 217
			}
		}
		add_to_array = { RUS.RUS_south_russian_states = THIS }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_rrf_state = yes				
				state = 221	
			}
		}		
		add_to_array = { RUS.RUS_psr_nrpr_buff_states = THIS }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 248		
				state = 573	
				state = 399
				state = 252
				state = 226
			}
		}		
		add_to_array = { RUS.RUS_psr_buff_states = THIS }
	}
}
RUS_recalculate_state_popularities = { #Fires monthly when elections are soon
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity_to_compare = 0.05 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity_to_compare = 0.06 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity_to_compare = 0.08 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity_to_compare = 0.08 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity_to_compare = 0.24 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity_to_compare = 0.15 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity_to_compare = 0.07 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity_to_compare = 0.04 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_popularity_to_compare = 0.06 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity_to_compare = 0.27 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity_to_compare = 0.27 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_divided_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_divided_popularity = 2 }
	
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity_to_compare = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity_to_compare = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity_to_compare = RUS_psr_rsdrp_divided_popularity }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity_to_compare = RUS_psr_rsdrp_divided_popularity }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity_to_compare = RUS.party_popularity@social_liberal }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity_to_compare = RUS.party_popularity@market_liberal }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity_to_compare = RUS.party_popularity@social_conservative }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity_to_compare = RUS.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity_to_compare = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity_to_compare = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = RUS_state_plsr_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = RUS_state_nsp_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = RUS_state_psr_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = RUS_state_vns_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = RUS_state_ep_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_popularity_to_compare }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_popularity_to_compare }
	
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: [?RUS_state_plsr_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_nsp_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_psr_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_lkdp_popularity_to_compare]"
	log = "[?RUS_state_rkdp_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_vns_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_ep_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_nrpr_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_nrpr_popularity_to_compare] - [?RUS_state_nsnp_popularity_to_compare]"
		
}
RUS_generate_state_popularities = { #Fires at game start, and when absorbing colonies
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@market_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@social_conservative }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 0.001 }
	
	#Adjust for PSR/RSDRP
	multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_popularity = 0.5 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 0.5 }
	
	#Adjust for ROVS
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_presidential_general_elections } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_popularity }
		
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction = 0.1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction = 0.4 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction = 0.25 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction = 0.25 }
		
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction }
	}	
		
	#Defining temporary state pop variables (to be reset by election)
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_popularity = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_popularity = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_socdem_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 1.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				NOT = { tag = TRM }
				NOT = { tag = DKB }
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				OR = {
					tag = TRM
					tag = DKB
				}
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_popularity = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_popularity = 1.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = national_populist
				NOT = { tag = TRM }
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = national_populist
				tag = TRM
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_popularity = 1.1 }
	}
	
	RUS_generate_special_state_popularities = yes
	
}
RUS_adjusted_state_pops = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0.03 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0.06 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_socdem_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0.07 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 1.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 1.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0.08 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 1.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				NOT = { tag = TRM }
				NOT = { tag = DKB }
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				OR = {
					tag = TRM
					tag = DKB
				}
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 1.05 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = national_populist
				NOT = { tag = TRM }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OWNER = {
				has_government = national_populist
				tag = TRM
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 1.1 }
	}	
}
RUS_generate_special_state_popularities = {
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_condition_pop = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_condition_pop = 0 }
	
	#Industry makes states more leftist
	set_temp_variable = { industrial_popularity = THIS.num_of_factories }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 10 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.25 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0.7 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 9 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.20 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0.75 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 8 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0.8 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 7 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0.85 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.15 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 6 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 5 }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0.95 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.05 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 4 }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 1.0 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 3 }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.95 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { industrial_popularity > 2 }
		}
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.9 }
	}
	### Urban Buff ###
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = one }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.25 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 1.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 1.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop = 1.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.75 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = two }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.6 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.6 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = three }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.7 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.7 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.85 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = four }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.8 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.8 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.9 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = five }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 0.95 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = six }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop = 1.1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = seven }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_condition_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.05 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.9 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.9 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = eight }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_condition_pop = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.8 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.8 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = nine }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.15 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_condition_pop = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.15 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.7 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.7 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = ten }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.2 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_condition_pop = 1.4 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.2 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.6 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.6 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = eleven }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.25 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 1.45 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 1.45 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_condition_pop = 1.45 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.25 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.55 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.55 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = twelve }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 0.3 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop = 1.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 1.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_ep_condition_pop = 1.45 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop = 1.3 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_condition_pop = 0.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop = 0.5 }
	}
	### Minorities ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 215
				state = 216
				state = 401
				state = 236
				state = 1197
				state = 1199
				state = 256
				state = 1193
				state = 399
				state = 397
				state = 651
				state = 1194
				state = 880
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_condition_pop = 0.5 }
	}
	### Oblastiniki buff ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_siberia = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_condition_pop = 0.5 }
	}
	### South Russia Buff ###
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 265
				state = 239
				state = 250
				state = 401
				state = 217
			}
		}	
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop = 0.25 }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_condition_pop = 0.25 }
	}
	RUS_get_final_popularities = yes
}
RUS_get_final_popularities = {
	#Prevents modifiers from stacking endlessly
	
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@social_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@market_liberal }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@social_conservative }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
	set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_independent_popularity }

	#Adjust for PSR/RSDRP
	multiply_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = 0.5 }
	multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_pop = 0.5 }
	
	#Adjust for ROVS
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_presidential_general_elections } }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_final_pop }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_final_pop }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_final_pop }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_final_pop }
		
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction = 0.1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction = 0.4 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction = 0.25 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction = 0.25 }
		
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction }
	}	
	
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_pop = RUS_state_psr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_vns_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_ep_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_final_pop = RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_independent_temp_pop }
	
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkp_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_pop = RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsp_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_pop = RUS_state_psr_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_pop = RUS_state_vns_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_pop = RUS_state_ep_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_condition_pop }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_pop = RUS_state_independent_condition_pop }
}

	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsp_senate_regional_votes = RUS_nsp_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_psr_senate_regional_votes = RUS_psr_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rsdrp_senate_regional_votes = RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_lkdp_senate_regional_votes = RUS_lkdp_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rkdp_senate_regional_votes = RUS_rkdp_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_vns_senate_regional_votes = RUS_vns_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_ep_senate_regional_votes = RUS_ep_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nrpr_senate_regional_votes = RUS_nrpr_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_senate_regional_votes = RUS_nsnp_senate_state_regional_vote }
	add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_independent_senate_regional_votes = RUS_independent_senate_state_regional_vote }
	
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR ([?RUS_plsr_senate_state_regional_vote]) - NSP ([?RUS_nsp_senate_state_regional_vote]) - PSR ([?RUS_psr_senate_state_regional_vote]) - RSDRP ([?RUS_rsdrp_senate_state_regional_vote]) - LKDP ([?RUS_lkdp_senate_state_regional_vote]) - RKDP ([?RUS_rkdp_senate_state_regional_vote]) - VNS ([?RUS_vns_senate_state_regional_vote])"
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: EP ([?RUS_ep_senate_state_regional_vote]) - NRPR ([?RUS_nrpr_senate_state_regional_vote]) - IND ([?RUS_independent_senate_state_regional_vote])"
}
	
RUS_calculate_polling_averages = {
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_poll_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@totalist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@social_liberal }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@market_liberal }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@social_conservative }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop = RUS.party_popularity@national_populist }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop = 0.001 }
		#Adjust for PSR/RSDRP
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop = 0.5 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop = 0.5 }
		
		#Adjust for ROVS
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_presidential_general_elections } }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_final_poll_pop }
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_final_poll_pop }
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_final_poll_pop }
			set_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction = RUS_state_rovs_final_poll_pop }
			
			multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction = 0.1 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction = 0.4 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction = 0.25 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction = 0.25 }
			
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rovs_rkdp_fraction }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rovs_vns_fraction }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rovs_ep_fraction }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rovs_nrpr_fraction }
		}	

		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_psr_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_vns_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_ep_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_independent_temp_pop }
		
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rkp_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_plsr_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nsp_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_psr_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rsdrp_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_lkdp_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_rkdp_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_vns_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_ep_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nrpr_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_nsnp_condition_pop }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop = RUS_state_independent_condition_pop }

		set_variable = { RUS_poll_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_poll_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_poll_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_poll_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_poll_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_poll_votes = RUS_poll_vote_count_state }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_vns_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_ep_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_poll_votes
		round_variable = RUS_independent_state_poll_votes

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_psr_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_vns_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_ep_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_independent_state_poll_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_poll_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		set_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_plsr_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_nsp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_psr_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_vns_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_ep_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_poll_votes = RUS_independent_state_poll_votes }

		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_plsr_poll_votes = RUS_plsr_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsp_poll_votes = RUS_nsp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_psr_poll_votes = RUS_psr_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_vns_poll_votes = RUS_vns_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_ep_poll_votes = RUS_ep_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_independent_poll_votes = RUS_independent_state_poll_votes }
		
		#log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR ([?RUS_plsr_state_poll_votes]) - NSP ([?RUS_nsp_state_poll_votes]) - PSR ([?RUS_psr_state_poll_votes]) - RSDRP ([?RUS_rsdrp_state_poll_votes]) - LKDP ([?RUS_lkdp_state_poll_votes]) - RKDP ([?RUS_rkdp_state_poll_votes]) - VNS ([?RUS_vns_state_poll_votes])"
		#log = "[THIS.GetName]: EP ([?RUS_ep_state_poll_votes]) - NRPR ([?RUS_nrpr_state_poll_votes]) - IND ([?RUS_independent_state_poll_votes]) - TOTAL VOTES ([?RUS_total_state_poll_votes])"
	}
	round_variable = RUS_plsr_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsp_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_psr_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_vns_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_ep_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes
	round_variable = RUS_independent_poll_votes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }

	if = {

			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
