		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsnp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_independent_poll_votes }
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_parliament_barrier }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition } }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_poll_votes = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_poll_votes = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
	}
		
	# If below 5% fuck off 
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Coalition_Only_In_Name
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Coalition_Only_In_Name
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Republican_Party_Of_Russia }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = rus_election_1936 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_kdp_poll_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_kdp_poll_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_poll_votes = 0 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = vns_ep_mp }
		set_variable = { vns_ep_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Republican_Party_Of_Russia }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_poll_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_poll_votes = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_poll_votes = 0 }
	}	
	
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rkdp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsnp_poll_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_independent_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_rsdrp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_kdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_psr_kdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_kdp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_kdp_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_kdp_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_vns_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_ep_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_rpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_rpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nrpr_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_rrdo_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_psr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_rrdo_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_lkdp_poll_votes }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_socialists_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_plsr_poll_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_socialists_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_nsp_poll_votes }
	
	divide_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_wide_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_popular_front_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_rsdrp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_kdp_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_kdp_vns_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rpr_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rrdo_percentage_poll_vote = RUS_total_poll_votes }
	
}
RUS_run_election = {
	RUS_clear_election_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rkdp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_vns_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_ep_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nrpr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_independent_state_votes

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		set_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_plsr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nsp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_psr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_vns_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_ep_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_independent_state_votes }

		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_plsr_votes = RUS_plsr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsp_votes = RUS_nsp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_psr_votes = RUS_psr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rsdrp_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_lkdp_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rkdp_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_vns_votes = RUS_vns_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_ep_votes = RUS_ep_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nrpr_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_independent_votes = RUS_independent_state_votes }

		
		#Resetting temp popularity
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }

		log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR ([?RUS_plsr_state_votes]) - NSP ([?RUS_nsp_state_votes]) - PSR ([?RUS_psr_state_votes]) - RSDRP ([?RUS_rsdrp_state_votes]) - LKDP ([?RUS_lkdp_state_votes]) - RKDP ([?RUS_rkdp_state_votes]) - VNS ([?RUS_vns_state_votes])"
		log = "[THIS.GetName]: EP ([?RUS_ep_state_votes]) - NRPR ([?RUS_nrpr_state_votes]) - IND ([?RUS_independent_state_votes]) - TOTAL VOTES ([?RUS_total_state_votes])"
	}
	round_variable = RUS_plsr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_psr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_lkdp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rkdp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_vns_votes
	round_variable = RUS_ep_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nrpr_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsnp_votes
	round_variable = RUS_independent_votes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = vns_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = ep_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nsnp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_ep_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nrpr_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsnp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_independent_votes }
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_total_votes }
	multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_parliament_barrier = RUS_parliament_barrier }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	add_to_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition } }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_votes = RUS_ep_votes }
	}
		
	# If below 5% fuck off 
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Coalition_Only_In_Name
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_plsr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
			has_completed_focus = RUS_Coalition_Only_In_Name
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_psr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Republican_Party_Of_Russia }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_psr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = rus_election_1936 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_kdp_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_kdp_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_lkdp_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_rkdp_votes }
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_vns_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_ep_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_ep_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_vns_ep_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = vns_ep_mp }
		set_variable = { vns_ep_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Republican_Party_Of_Russia }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nrpr_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes < RUS_temp_parliament_barrier }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { RUS_total_votes = RUS_nsnp_votes }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	}
	
	
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_vote = RUS_plsr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_vote = RUS_nsp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_vote = RUS_psr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote = RUS_rsdrp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_lkdp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_rkdp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = RUS_vns_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_vote = RUS_ep_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote = RUS_nrpr_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote = RUS_nsnp_votes }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_vote = RUS_independent_votes }
	
	divide_variable = { RUS_plsr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_psr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_vns_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_ep_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_vote = RUS_total_votes }
	
	set_variable = { plsr_total_mp = RUS_plsr_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { nsp_total_mp = RUS_nsp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { psr_total_mp = RUS_psr_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp = RUS_rsdrp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { lkdp_total_mp = RUS_lkdp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { rkdp_total_mp = RUS_rkdp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { vns_total_mp = RUS_vns_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { ep_total_mp = RUS_ep_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { nrpr_total_mp = RUS_nrpr_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { nsnp_total_mp = RUS_nsnp_percentage_vote }
	set_variable = { independent_total_mp = RUS_independent_percentage_vote }
	
	multiply_variable = { plsr_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { nsp_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { psr_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { lkdp_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { rkdp_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { vns_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { ep_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { nrpr_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { nsnp_total_mp = 550 }
	multiply_variable = { independent_total_mp = 550 }
	
	round_variable = plsr_total_mp 
	round_variable = nsp_total_mp 
	round_variable = psr_total_mp 
	round_variable = rsdrp_total_mp 
	round_variable = lkdp_total_mp 
	round_variable = rkdp_total_mp 
	round_variable = vns_total_mp 
	round_variable = ep_total_mp 
	round_variable = nrpr_total_mp 
	round_variable = nsnp_total_mp 
	round_variable = independent_total_mp 
	
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = plsr_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = psr_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rsdrp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = lkdp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rkdp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = vns_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = ep_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nrpr_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsnp_total_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = independent_total_mp }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 550 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 553 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_mp = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 552 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_mp = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 551 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_mp = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 549 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_mp = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 548 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_mp = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 547 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_mp = 3 }
		}
	}
	
	set_variable = { plsr_mp = plsr_total_mp }
	set_variable = { nsp_mp = nsp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { psr_mp = psr_total_mp }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_mp = rsdrp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { lkdp_mp = lkdp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { rkdp_mp = rkdp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { vns_mp = vns_total_mp }
	set_variable = { ep_mp = ep_total_mp }
	set_variable = { nrpr_mp = nrpr_total_mp }
	set_variable = { nsnp_mp = nsnp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { independent_mp = independent_total_mp }
	
	# Count for coalitions
	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = rus_election_1936 } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition
			}
			set_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp = plsr_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp = nsnp_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp = psr_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp = rsdrp_total_mp }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition
			}
			set_variable = { popular_front_mp = plsr_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { popular_front_mp = nsp_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { popular_front_mp = rsdrp_total_mp }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { socialists_mp = plsr_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { socialists_mp = nsp_total_mp }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition
			}
			set_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp = psr_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp = rsdrp_total_mp }
		}
		set_variable = { kdp_mp = lkdp_total_mp }
		add_to_variable = { kdp_mp = rkdp_total_mp }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition
			}
			set_variable = { psr_kdp_mp = psr_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { psr_kdp_mp = kdp_mp }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition
			}
			set_variable = { kdp_vns_mp = kdp_mp }
			add_to_variable = { kdp_vns_mp = vns_total_mp }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition }
			}
			set_variable = { vns_ep_mp = vns_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { vns_ep_mp = ep_total_mp }
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { socialists_mp = 0 }
		set_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp = 0 }
		set_variable = { popular_front_mp = 0 }
		set_variable = { psr_kdp_mp = 0 }
		set_variable = { kdp_vns_mp = 0 }
		set_variable = { vns_ep_mp = 0 }
		set_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties
			}
			set_variable = { rrdo_mp = psr_mp }
			add_to_variable = { rrdo_mp = lkdp_mp }
			set_variable = { kdp_mp = rkdp_total_mp }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = { kdp_mp = lkdp_total_mp }
			add_to_variable = { kdp_mp = rkdp_total_mp }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Republican_Party_Of_Russia
			}
			set_variable = { rpr_mp = psr_mp }
			add_to_variable = { rpr_mp = nrpr_mp }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { wide_popular_front_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_wide_popular_front_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { popular_front_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_popular_front_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_rsdrp_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_psr_rsdrp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_psr_kdp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_vns_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_kdp_vns_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_ep_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_vns_ep_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { socialists_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_socialists_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > rpr_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > rrdo_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > lkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > rkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { plsr_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = rus_election_1936
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_plsr_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > rpr_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > rrdo_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > lkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > rkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsp_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = rus_election_1936
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_nsp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_psr_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > rrdo_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > rpr_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_rsdrp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_wide_popular_front_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_popular_front_coalition }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_rsdrp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { rrdo_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rrdo_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rrdo_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rrdo_mp > rkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rrdo_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rrdo_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rrdo_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rrdo_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_rrdo_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { rpr_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rpr_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rpr_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rpr_mp > lkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rpr_mp > rkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rpr_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rpr_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rpr_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_rpr_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > rpr_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { kdp_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_kdp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > rpr_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > rkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { lkdp_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = rus_election_1936
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_lkdp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > rpr_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > rrdo_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > lkdp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { rkdp_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			has_country_flag = rus_election_1936
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_rkdp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > rrdo_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > rpr_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition }

		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_vns_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > rrdo_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > rpr_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }

			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > popular_front_mp }

			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > rrdo_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > vns_ep_mp }

			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
		}

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > rrdo_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > kdp_vns_mp }

			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }

	}		
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_PLSR_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_NSP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_RSDRP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_PSR_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_LKDP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_RKDP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_VNS_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_EP_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_NRPR_CAMPAIGN
	clr_country_flag = RUS_1941_NSNP_CAMPAIGN
	round_variable = RUS_total_votes
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR([?plsr_total_mp]) - NSP([?nsp_total_mp]) - RSDRP([?rsdrp_total_mp]) - PSR([?psr_total_mp]) - KDP([?kdp_mp])"
	log = "VNS([?vns_total_mp]) - EP([?ep_total_mp]) - NRPR([?nrpr_total_mp]) - NSNP([?nsnp_total_mp]) - IND([?independent_total_mp])"
	mp_support_calc = yes
	RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = yes
}

RUS_run_senate_election = {
	RUS_clear_senate_election_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
		
	set_variable = { RUS_total_senate_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_total_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes
		
		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_senate_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_senate_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_senate_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_state_senate_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_state_senate_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_state_senate_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes = RUS_nonconservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_senate_votes = RUS_conservative_senate_state_turnout }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_vns_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_ep_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes
		round_variable = RUS_independent_state_senate_votes

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {

				check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_vns_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_ep_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_independent_state_senate_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_senate_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		RUS_get_regional_senators = yes
		
		set_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_psr_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_vns_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_ep_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_senate_votes = RUS_independent_state_senate_votes }

		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_plsr_senate_votes = RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsp_senate_votes = RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_psr_senate_votes = RUS_psr_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_lkdp_senate_votes = RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_rkdp_senate_votes = RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_vns_senate_votes = RUS_vns_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_ep_senate_votes = RUS_ep_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nrpr_senate_votes = RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_nsnp_senate_votes = RUS_nsnp_state_senate_votes }
		add_to_variable = { PREV.RUS_independent_senate_votes = RUS_independent_state_senate_votes }

		
		#Resetting temp popularity
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_rovs_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = 0 }

		log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR ([?RUS_plsr_state_senate_votes]) - NSP ([?RUS_nsp_state_senate_votes]) - PSR ([?RUS_psr_state_senate_votes]) - RSDRP ([?RUS_rsdrp_state_senate_votes]) - LKDP ([?RUS_lkdp_state_senate_votes]) - RKDP ([?RUS_rkdp_state_senate_votes]) - VNS ([?RUS_vns_state_senate_votes])"
		log = "[THIS.GetName]: EP ([?RUS_ep_state_senate_votes]) - NRPR ([?RUS_nrpr_state_senate_votes]) - IND ([?RUS_independent_state_senate_votes]) - TOTAL senate_votes ([?RUS_total_state_senate_votes])"
	}
	round_variable = RUS_plsr_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_psr_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_lkdp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_rkdp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_vns_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_ep_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nrpr_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_nsnp_senate_votes
	round_variable = RUS_independent_senate_votes
	
	#Adjust for banned parties
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = nrpr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = psr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = bolsheviks_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = rsdrp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = plsr_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_senate_regional_votes = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			RUS = { has_country_flag = lkdp_banned }
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_votes = 0 }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_senate_regional_votes = 0 }

	set_variable = { lkdp_total_regional_senators = RUS_lkdp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
	set_variable = { rkdp_total_regional_senators = RUS_rkdp_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
	set_variable = { vns_total_regional_senators = RUS_vns_percentage_senate_regional_vote }
	set_variable = { ep_total_regional_senators = RUS_ep_percentage_senate_regional_vote }

	set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = ep_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nrpr_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsnp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = independent_total_regional_senators }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = senators_election_regional_total }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_3 = senators_election_regional_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_3 = 3 }
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = RUS_deputy_var_checker_3 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_2 = senators_election_regional_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_2 = 2 }
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = RUS_deputy_var_checker_2 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_1 = senators_election_regional_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_1 = 1 }
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = RUS_deputy_var_checker_1 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_1 = senators_election_regional_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_1 = -1 }
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = RUS_deputy_var_checker_1 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_senators = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_2 = senators_election_regional_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_2 = -2 }
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = RUS_deputy_var_checker_2 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_senators = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_3 = senators_election_regional_total }
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker_3 = -3 }
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = RUS_deputy_var_checker_3 }

	}

	set_variable = { nsp_regional_senators = nsp_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { psr_regional_senators = psr_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_regional_senators = rsdrp_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { lkdp_regional_senators = lkdp_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { rkdp_regional_senators = rkdp_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { vns_regional_senators = vns_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { ep_regional_senators = ep_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { nrpr_regional_senators = nrpr_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { nsnp_regional_senators = nsnp_total_regional_senators }
	set_variable = { independent_regional_senators = independent_total_regional_senators }
	
	
	set_variable = { kdp_total_regional_senators = lkdp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { kdp_total_regional_senators = rkdp_total_regional_senators }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators > nsp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators > psr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators > rsdrp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators > kdp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators > vns_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators > ep_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators > nrpr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { plsr_total_regional_senators > nsnp_total_regional_senators }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_SENATE_REGION_plsr_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators > plsr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators > psr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators > rsdrp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators > kdp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators > vns_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators > ep_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators > nrpr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsp_total_regional_senators > nsnp_total_regional_senators }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_SENATE_REGION_nsp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators > plsr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators > nsp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators > rsdrp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators > kdp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators > vns_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators > ep_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators > nrpr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { psr_total_regional_senators > nsnp_total_regional_senators }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_SENATE_REGION_psr_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators > plsr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators > nsp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators > psr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators > kdp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators > vns_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators > ep_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators > nrpr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { rsdrp_total_regional_senators > nsnp_total_regional_senators }

			check_variable = { kdp_total_regional_senators > plsr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { kdp_total_regional_senators > nsp_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { kdp_total_regional_senators > psr_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { kdp_total_regional_senators > rsdrp_total_regional_senators }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { ep_total_regional_senators > plsr_total_regional_senators }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_regional_senators > plsr_total_regional_senators }

			check_variable = { nsnp_total_regional_senators > vns_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_regional_senators > ep_total_regional_senators }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_regional_senators > nrpr_total_regional_senators }

	}
	round_variable = RUS_total_senate_regional_votes
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: (Regional) PLSR([?plsr_total_regional_senators]) - NSP([?nsp_total_regional_senators]) - RSDRP([?rsdrp_total_regional_senators]) - PSR([?psr_total_regional_senators]) - KDP([?kdp_mp])"
	log = "VNS([?vns_total_regional_senators]) - EP([?ep_total_regional_senators]) - NRPR([?nrpr_total_regional_senators]) - NSNP([?nsnp_total_regional_senators]) - IND([?independent_total_regional_senators])"
}
RUS_run_1937_election = {
	RUS_clear_election_variables = yes
	set_variable = { RUS_rkp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rovs_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_pop }
		
		divide_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = 2 }
		divide_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = 2 }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rkdp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_vns_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_ep_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nrpr_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_votes
		round_variable = RUS_independent_state_votes

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_votes = 0 }
		}	
		
		set_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_plsr_state_votes }

		add_to_variable = { RUS_total_state_votes = RUS_psr_state_votes }

			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { psr_kdp_mp > nsnp_total_mp }

			check_variable = { kdp_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = democratic_block_coalition }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_kdp_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > dem_block_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { vns_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_vns_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > dem_block_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { ep_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_ep_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > dem_block_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nrpr_total_mp > nsnp_total_mp }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_nrpr_victory
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > plsr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > nsp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > socialists_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > wide_popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > popular_front_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > psr_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > rsdrp_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > psr_rsdrp_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > psr_kdp_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > dem_block_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > kdp_vns_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > vns_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > vns_ep_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > ep_total_mp }
			check_variable = { nsnp_total_mp > nrpr_total_mp }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ELECTION_nsnp_victory
	}
	round_variable = RUS_total_votes
	log = "[THIS.GetName]: PLSR([?plsr_total_mp]) - NSP([?nsp_total_mp]) - RSDRP([?rsdrp_total_mp]) - PSR([?psr_total_mp]) - KDP([?kdp_mp])"
	log = "VNS([?vns_total_mp]) - EP([?ep_total_mp]) - NRPR([?nrpr_total_mp]) - NSNP([?nsnp_total_mp]) - IND([?independent_total_mp])"
	mp_support_calc = yes
	RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = yes
}

RUS_run_presidential_elections = {
	RUS_clear_president_election_variables = yes
	set_country_flag = RUS_presidential_general_elections

	set_variable = { RUS_plsr_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsp_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_psr_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_vns_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_ep_president_votes = 0 }

	set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_president_votes = 0 }
	set_variable = { RUS_independent_president_votes = 0 }
	
	set_variable = { RUS_total_president_votes = 0 }
	
	every_owned_state = {
		RUS_get_final_popularities = yes

		set_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = state_population_k }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vote_count_state = RUS_state_general_turnout }

		set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_president_votes = RUS_state_plsr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_president_votes = RUS_state_nsp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_psr_state_president_votes = RUS_state_psr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_president_votes = RUS_state_rsdrp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_president_votes = RUS_state_lkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_president_votes = RUS_state_rkdp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_vns_state_president_votes = RUS_state_vns_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_ep_state_president_votes = RUS_state_ep_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_president_votes = RUS_state_nrpr_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_president_votes = RUS_state_nsnp_final_pop }
		set_variable = { RUS_independent_state_president_votes = RUS_state_independent_final_pop }

		multiply_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_psr_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rsdrp_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_lkdp_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_vns_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_ep_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nrpr_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_nsnp_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_independent_state_president_votes = RUS_vote_count_state }

		round_variable = RUS_plsr_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsp_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_psr_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rsdrp_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_lkdp_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_rkdp_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_vns_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_ep_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nrpr_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_nsnp_state_president_votes
		round_variable = RUS_independent_state_president_votes

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_president_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_plsr_state_president_votes = 0 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_president_votes < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_nsp_state_president_votes = 0 }
		}

				check_variable = { RUS_rkdp_state_president_votes < 0 }

		if = {

	divide_variable = { RUS_nrpr_percentage_president_vote = RUS_total_president_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_nsnp_percentage_president_vote = RUS_total_president_votes }
	divide_variable = { RUS_independent_percentage_president_vote = RUS_total_president_votes }
	
	
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Unite_The_Parties
			}
			set_variable = { RUS_rrdo_percentage_president_vote = RUS_psr_percentage_president_vote }

		}
