mp_support_calc = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition
				plsr_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { plsr_mp = plsr_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { plsr_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition
				nsp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nsp_mp = nsp_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { nsp_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition
				rsdrp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { rsdrp_mp = rsdrp_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { rsdrp_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = psr_coalition
				psr_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { psr_mp = psr_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { psr_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition
				lkdp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { lkdp_mp = lkdp_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { lkdp_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition
				rkdp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { rkdp_mp = rkdp_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { rkdp_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition
				vns_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { vns_mp = vns_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { vns_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ep_mp = ep_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ep_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = national_populist_coalition
				has_idea = RUS_Boris_V_Savinkov_hog_npo
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nrpr_mp = nrpr_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { nrpr_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = solidarist_coalition
				nsnp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nsnp_mp = nsnp_total_mp }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { nsnp_mp = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = independent_coalition
			}
		}
		set_variable = { independent_mp = 0 }
	}

	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = plsr_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nsp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = rsdrp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = psr_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = lkdp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = rkdp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = vns_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = ep_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nrpr_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nsnp_mp }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = independent_mp }
	set_variable = { mp_support = temp1 }
}
senators_support_calc = {
	final_senators_recalc = yes
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = syndicalist_coalition
				plsr_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { plsr_senators_support = plsr_final_senators }
		set_variable = { plsr_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { plsr_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { plsr_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = radical_socialist_coalition
				nsp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nsp_senators_support = nsp_final_senators }
		set_variable = { nsp_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { nsp_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { nsp_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = rsdrp_coalition
				rsdrp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { rsdrp_senators_support = rsdrp_final_senators }
		set_variable = { rsdrp_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { rsdrp_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { rsdrp_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = psr_coalition
				psr_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { psr_senators_support = psr_final_senators }
		set_variable = { psr_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { psr_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { psr_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = social_liberal_coalition
				lkdp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { lkdp_senators_support = lkdp_final_senators }
		set_variable = { lkdp_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { lkdp_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { lkdp_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition
				rkdp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { rkdp_senators_support = rkdp_final_senators }
		set_variable = { rkdp_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { rkdp_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { rkdp_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = social_conservative_coalition
				vns_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { vns_senators_support = vns_final_senators }
		set_variable = { vns_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { vns_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { vns_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = authoritarian_democrat_coalition
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ep_senators_support = ep_final_senators }
		set_variable = { ep_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { ep_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ep_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = national_populist_coalition
				has_idea = RUS_Boris_V_Savinkov_hog_npo
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nrpr_senators_support = nrpr_final_senators }
		set_variable = { nrpr_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { nrpr_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { ep_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = solidarist_coalition
				nsnp_in_power = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { nsnp_senators_support = nsnp_final_senators }
		set_variable = { nsnp_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { nsnp_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { nsnp_senators_support = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = independent_coalition
			}
		}
		set_variable = { independent_senators = 0 }
		set_variable = { independent_regional_senators = 0 }
	}
	
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = plsr_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nsp_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = rsdrp_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = psr_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = lkdp_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = rkdp_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = vns_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = ep_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nrpr_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = nsnp_senators_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp1 = independent_senators_support }
	
	set_variable = { senate_support = temp1 }
}
final_senators_recalc = {
	set_variable = { plsr_final_senators = plsr_total_senators }
	set_variable = { nsp_final_senators = nsp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_final_senators = rsdrp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { psr_final_senators = psr_total_senators }
	set_variable = { lkdp_final_senators = lkdp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { rkdp_final_senators = rkdp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { vns_final_senators = vns_total_senators }
	set_variable = { ep_final_senators = ep_total_senators }
	set_variable = { nrpr_final_senators = nrpr_total_senators }
	set_variable = { nsnp_final_senators = nsnp_total_senators }
	set_variable = { independent_final_senators = independent_total_senators }
	
	add_to_variable = { plsr_final_senators = plsr_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nsp_final_senators = nsp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { rsdrp_final_senators = rsdrp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { psr_final_senators = psr_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { lkdp_final_senators = lkdp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { rkdp_final_senators = rkdp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { vns_final_senators = vns_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { ep_final_senators = ep_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nrpr_final_senators = nrpr_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nsnp_final_senators = nsnp_total_regional_senators }
	add_to_variable = { independent_final_senators = independent_total_regional_senators }
	
	### Adding presidential senators
	add_to_variable = { plsr_final_senators = plsr_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nsp_final_senators = nsp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { rsdrp_final_senators = rsdrp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { psr_final_senators = psr_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { lkdp_final_senators = lkdp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { rkdp_final_senators = rkdp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { vns_final_senators = vns_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { ep_final_senators = ep_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nrpr_final_senators = nrpr_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { nsnp_final_senators = nsnp_presidential_senators }
	add_to_variable = { independent_final_senators = independent_presidential_senators }
	

	set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = plsr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rsdrp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = psr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = lkdp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rkdp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = vns_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = ep_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nrpr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsnp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = independent_final_senators }

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 150 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 153 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 152 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 151 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 149 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_senators = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 148 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_senators = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 147 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_senators = 3 }
		}
	}
}

RUS_increase_plsr_pop = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_plsr_pop_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_plsr_temp_pop = 0.1 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_psr_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rsdrp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_lkdp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_rkdp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_vns_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_ep_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nrpr_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_nsnp_temp_pop = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { RUS_state_independent_temp_pop = -0.01 }
		}
	}
	add_popularity = {
		ideology = syndicalist
		popularity = 0.07
	}
}

RUS_Get_Lower_House_Array = {
	# Generate partial sums t1 = (P1), t2 = (P1 + P2), t3 = (P1 + P2 + P3)
	
	# so that we can use resize_array to fill our array with the right number of seats for each party
	set_temp_variable = { t1 = plsr_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t2 = nsp_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t3 = psr_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t4 = rsdrp_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t5 = lkdp_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t6 = rkdp_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t7 = vns_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t8 = ep_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t9 = nsnp_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t10 = nrpr_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t11 = independent_total_mp }
	set_temp_variable = { t12 = 550 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { t2 = t1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t3 = t2 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t4 = t3 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t5 = t4 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t6 = t5 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t7 = t6 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t8 = t7 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t9 = t8 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t10 = t9 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t11 = t10 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t12 = t11 }
	
	clear_array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
	
	# Resize array to t1 seats, setting P1 frame numbers to 1 (Party 1 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 1
		size = t1
	}
	# Resize array to t2 seats, setting P2 frame numbers to 2 (Party 2 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 2
		size = t2
	}
	# Resize array to t3 seats, setting P3 frame numbers to 3 (Party 3 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 3
		size = t3
	}
	# Resize array to t4 seats, setting P3 frame numbers to 3 (Party 3 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 4
		size = t4
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 5
		size = t5
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 6
		size = t6
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 7
		size = t7
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 8
		size = t8
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 9
		size = t9
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 10
		size = t10
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 11
		size = t11
	}
	# Resize array to all 550 seats, setting remaining frame numbers to 11 (Party 11 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Lower_House_Display
		value = 12
		size = t12
	}
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: DUMA ARRAY LENGHT [?RUS_Lower_House_Display^num]"
}
RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = {
	# Generate partial sums t1 = (P1), t2 = (P1 + P2), t3 = (P1 + P2 + P3)
	
	# so that we can use resize_array to fill our array with the right number of seats for each party
	set_temp_variable = { t1 = plsr_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t2 = nsp_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t3 = psr_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t4 = rsdrp_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t5 = lkdp_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t6 = rkdp_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t7 = vns_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t8 = ep_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t9 = nsnp_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t10 = nrpr_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t11 = independent_final_senators }
	set_temp_variable = { t12 = 150 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { t2 = t1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t3 = t2 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t4 = t3 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t5 = t4 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t6 = t5 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t7 = t6 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t8 = t7 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t9 = t8 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t10 = t9 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t11 = t10 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { t12 = t11 }
	
	clear_array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
	
	# Resize array to t1 seats, setting P1 frame numbers to 1 (Party 1 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 1
		size = t1
	}
	# Resize array to t2 seats, setting P2 frame numbers to 2 (Party 2 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 2
		size = t2
	}
	# Resize array to t3 seats, setting P3 frame numbers to 3 (Party 3 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 3
		size = t3
	}
	# Resize array to t4 seats, setting P3 frame numbers to 3 (Party 3 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 4
		size = t4
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 5
		size = t5
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 6
		size = t6
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 7
		size = t7
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 8
		size = t8
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 9
		size = t9
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 10
		size = t10
	}
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 11
		size = t11
	}
	# Resize array to all 150 seats, setting remaining frame numbers to 11 (Party 11 color)
	resize_array = {
		array = RUS_Senate_Election_Display
		value = 12
		size = t12
	}
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: SENATE ARRAY LENGHT [?RUS_Senate_Election_Display^num]"
	set_variable = { three_fifth_of_senate = 90 }
}

predetermine_all_presidential_candidates = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NSP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = NSP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = PSR_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {	
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = EP_candidate_existed
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_exists
		}
		set_country_flag = NSP_candidate_existed
	}
}
restore_all_presidential_candidates = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_existed
		}
		set_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_existed
		}

}

		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }

			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
				check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }

				check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
				check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }

			clr_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists

count_second_tour_candidates = {
	set_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = 0 }
	set_variable = { votes_for_vns_candidate = 0 }
		
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_exists }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = plsr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = nsp_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = psr_final_senators }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = vernadsky_ep_candidate
							has_country_flag = savitsky_ep_candidate
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate = nrpr_final_senators }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NSP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = plsr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = nsp_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = psr_final_senators }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = vernadsky_ep_candidate
							has_country_flag = savitsky_ep_candidate
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate = nrpr_final_senators }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = plsr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = nsp_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = psr_final_senators }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = vernadsky_ep_candidate
							has_country_flag = savitsky_ep_candidate
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = nrpr_final_senators }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = plsr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = nsp_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = psr_final_senators }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
							has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = lkdp_final_senators }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
							has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
						}
					}
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition
							has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
							has_country_flag = VNS_candidate_exists
							has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = rkdp_final_senators }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = vernadsky_ep_candidate
							has_country_flag = savitsky_ep_candidate
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = nrpr_final_senators }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = 0 }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = plsr_final_senators }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = nsp_final_senators }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_psr_kdp_coalition }
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = psr_final_senators }
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = lkdp_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
					}
				}
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition
						has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = VNS_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = rkdp_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = vernadsky_ep_candidate
						has_country_flag = savitsky_ep_candidate
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = nrpr_final_senators }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = lkdp_final_senators }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = rkdp_final_senators }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = vns_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = VNS_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = ep_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = NSP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = psr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = lkdp_final_senators }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = rkdp_final_senators }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = vns_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = VNS_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = ep_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = NSP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = psr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = lkdp_final_senators }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = rkdp_final_senators }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = vns_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = VNS_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = ep_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = NSP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = psr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Conservative_candidate_exists
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = vns_final_senators }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = lkdp_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = rkdp_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = ep_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = vernadsky_ep_candidate
					has_country_flag = savitsky_ep_candidate
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = nrpr_final_senators }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate = ep_final_senators }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = NRPR_candidate_exists
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = nrpr_final_senators }
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = ep_final_senators }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Socialist_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = NSP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PLSR_candidate_exists
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = plsr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = nsp_final_senators }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
						has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = Liberal_candidate_exists
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = teslenko_kdp_candidate
								has_country_flag = teslenko_vns_kdp_candidate
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = psr_final_senators }
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = rsdrp_final_senators }
		}
	}
	
	
			
	
	### Independent Candidates Vote For Ruling###
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			psr_in_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = maklakov_psr_kdp_candidate
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			rsdrp_in_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_liberal
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition
				NOT = { has_country_flag = teslenko_vns_kdp_candidate }
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
			}
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate = independent_final_senators }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = national_populist
		}
		add_to_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate = independent_final_senators }
	}
	
}	
RUS_determine_president_winner = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_conservative_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_liberal_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_lkdp_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_LKDP_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rkdp_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_RKDP_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nsp_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_NSP_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_plsr_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_PLSR_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_psr_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_PSR_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_rsdrp_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_RSDRP_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_socialist_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_ep_candidate > votes_for_nrpr_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_EP_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_conservative_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_liberal_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_lkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_rkdp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_nsp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_plsr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_psr_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_rsdrp_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_ep_candidate }
			check_variable = { votes_for_nrpr_candidate > votes_for_socialist_candidate }
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_NRPR_Candidate_Winner
	}
}
setup_presidential_government_senate = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Dmitriy Romanov"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible }
			}
			load_base_russian_tree = yes
			set_country_flag = make_russia_liberal_conservative_democratic_tree_visible
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes

setup_ruling_party_president = {
	clr_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_LKDP_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_RKDP_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_PLSR_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_NSP_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_RSDRP_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_PSR_Candidate_Winner
	clr_country_flag = RUS_NRPR_Candidate_Winner
	restore_all_presidential_candidates = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			psr_in_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = maklakov_psr_kdp_candidate
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = PSR_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_PSR_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			rsdrp_in_power = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RSDRP_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_RSDRP_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government = social_liberal
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = LKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_LKDP_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RKDP_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_RKDP_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_kdp_vns_coalition
				NOT = { has_country_flag = teslenko_vns_kdp_candidate }
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EP_candidate_exists
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_EP_Candidate_Winner
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = national_populist
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_NRPR_Candidate_Winner
	}
	setup_new_president = yes
}
setup_new_president = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_Conservative_Candidate_Winner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = vernadsky_ep_candidate		
				}
				RUS_setup_president_vernadskiy = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = savitsky_ep_candidate		
				}
				RUS_setup_president_savitskiy = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = yusupov_vns_kdp_candidate
						has_country_flag = yusupov_vns_candidate
					}
				}
				RUS_setup_president_yusupov = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_romanov = yes
			}			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_Liberal_Candidate_Winner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = maklakov_psr_kdp_candidate
						has_country_flag = maklakov_kdp_candidate
					}
				}
				RUS_setup_president_maklakov = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = teslenko_kdp_candidate
						has_country_flag = teslenko_vns_kdp_candidate
					}		
				}
				RUS_setup_president_teslenko = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_tereschenko = yes
			}			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_PSR_Candidate_Winner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = gershtein_psr_candidate
				}
				RUS_setup_president_gershtein = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = avksentiev_psr_candidate	
						has_country_flag = avksentiev_psr_kdp_candidate
					}
				}
				RUS_setup_president_avksentiev = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_chernov = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_RSDRP_Candidate_Winner
			}
			RUS_setup_president_lozovskiy = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_Socialist_Candidate_Winner
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = gershtein_psr_candidate
				}
				RUS_setup_president_gershtein = yes
			}
			else = {
				RUS_setup_president_lozovskiy = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_NRPR_Candidate_Winner
			}
			RUS_setup_president_odinets = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SENATE_RSDRP_REFORM_accepted }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SENATE_NSP_REFORM_accepted }
			}
			remove_add_presidential_senators = yes
		}
	}
}
remove_add_presidential_senators = {
	set_variable = { plsr_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nsp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { rsdrp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { lkdp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { rkdp_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { vns_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { ep_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { nrpr_presidential_senators = 0 }
	set_variable = { independent_presidential_senators = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_vns_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { vns_presidential_senators = 40 }
		set_variable = { ep_presidential_senators = 5 }
		set_variable = { rkdp_presidential_senators = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_ep_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { ep_presidential_senators = 50 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_rkdp_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { rkdp_presidential_senators = 40 }		
		set_variable = { lkdp_presidential_senators = 10 }		
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_lkdp_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { lkdp_presidential_senators = 40 }
		set_variable = { rkdp_presidential_senators = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_psr_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 50 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_rsdrp_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { rsdrp_presidential_senators = 50 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Lev Gershtein"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 25 }
		set_variable = { rsdrp_presidential_senators = 15 }
		set_variable = { nsp_presidential_senators = 5 }
		set_variable = { plsr_presidential_senators = 5 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Solomon Lozovskiy"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { rsdrp_presidential_senators = 25 }
		set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 5 }
		set_variable = { nsp_presidential_senators = 5 }
		set_variable = { plsr_presidential_senators = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_nrpr_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { nrpr_presidential_senators = 50 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_nsnp_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { nsnp_presidential_senators = 50 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_nsp_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { nsp_presidential_senators = 50 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_a_plsr_president = yes
		}
		set_variable = { plsr_presidential_senators = 50 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Pitirim Sorokin"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = democratic_block_coalition }
			}
			set_variable = { vns_presidential_senators = 20 }
			set_variable = { independent_presidential_senators = 20 }
			set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 10 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = democratic_block_coalition
			}
			set_variable = { lkdp_presidential_senators = 15 }
			set_variable = { rsdrp_presidential_senators = 10 }
			set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 25 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_I_Was_Never_A_Socialist
			}
			set_variable = { lkdp_presidential_senators = 40 }
			set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 10 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_I_Was_Never_A_Liberal
			}
			set_variable = { rsdrp_presidential_senators = 20 }
			set_variable = { psr_presidential_senators = 30 }
		}		
	}
	
	final_senators_recalc = yes
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = 0 }

	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = plsr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rsdrp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = psr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = lkdp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = rkdp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = vns_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = ep_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nrpr_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = nsnp_final_senators }
	add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = independent_final_senators }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker = senate_total }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker > senate_total }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = senate_total }
			subtract_from_variable = { independent_total_senators = temp1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_deputy_var_checker < senate_total }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp1 = senate_total }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_deputy_var_checker }
			add_to_variable = { independent_total_senators = temp1 }
		}
	}
	senators_support_calc = yes
	RUS_Get_Senate_Elections_Array = yes
}

	set_variable = { CurrentPLSRSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentNSPSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentPSRSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentRSDRPSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentLKDPSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentRKDPSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentVNSSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentEPSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentNRPRSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentNSNPSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentPLSRSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentNSPSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentPSRSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentRSDRPSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentLKDPSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentRKDPSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentVNSSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentEPSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentNRPRSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentNSNPSenateSupportForBill = 0 }
}
RUS_LAW_calculate_support = {
	set_variable = { CurrentPLSRSupportForBill = plsr_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentNSPSupportForBill = nsp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentPSRSupportForBill = psr_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentRSDRPSupportForBill = rsdrp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentLKDPSupportForBill = lkdp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentRKDPSupportForBill = rkdp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentVNSSupportForBill = vns_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentEPSupportForBill = ep_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentNRPRSupportForBill = nrpr_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentNSNPSupportForBill = nsnp_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentIndependentSupportForBill = independent_total_mp }
	set_variable = { CurrentPLSRSenateSupportForBill = plsr_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentNSPSenateSupportForBill = nsp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentPSRSenateSupportForBill = psr_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentRSDRPSenateSupportForBill = rsdrp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentLKDPSenateSupportForBill = lkdp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentRKDPSenateSupportForBill = rkdp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentVNSSenateSupportForBill = vns_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentEPSenateSupportForBill = ep_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentNRPRSenateSupportForBill = nrpr_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentNSNPSenateSupportForBill = nsnp_final_senators }
	set_variable = { CurrentIndependentSenateSupportForBill = independent_final_senators }
	
	multiply_variable = { CurrentPLSRSupportForBill = CurrentPLSRSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentNSPSupportForBill = CurrentNSPSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentPSRSupportForBill = CurrentPSRSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentRSDRPSupportForBill = CurrentRSDRPSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentLKDPSupportForBill = CurrentLKDPSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentRKDPSupportForBill = CurrentRKDPSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentVNSSupportForBill = CurrentVNSSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentEPSupportForBill = CurrentEPSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentNRPRSupportForBill = CurrentNRPRSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentNSNPSupportForBill = CurrentNSNPSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentIndependentSupportForBill = CurrentIndependentSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentPLSRSenateSupportForBill = CurrentPLSRSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentNSPSenateSupportForBill = CurrentNSPSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentPSRSenateSupportForBill = CurrentPSRSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentRSDRPSenateSupportForBill = CurrentRSDRPSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentLKDPSenateSupportForBill = CurrentLKDPSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentRKDPSenateSupportForBill = CurrentRKDPSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentVNSSenateSupportForBill = CurrentVNSSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentEPSenateSupportForBill = CurrentEPSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentNRPRSenateSupportForBill = CurrentNRPRSenateSupportForBillPerc }
	multiply_variable = { CurrentNSNPSenateSupportForBill = CurrentNSNPSenateSupportForBillPerc }

	round_variable = CurrentNRPRSenateSupportForBill
	round_variable = CurrentNSNPSenateSupportForBill
	round_variable = CurrentIndependentSenateSupportForBill
	
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentPLSRSupportForBill }

	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentRSDRPSupportForBill }

			OR = {

				has_government = social_democrat
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentPLSRSupportForBillPerc = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { CurrentNSPSupportForBillPerc = 1 }

count_votes_for_bill_sum = {
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentPLSRSupportForBill min = 0 max = plsr_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentNSPSupportForBill min = 0 max = nsp_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentPSRSupportForBill min = 0 max = psr_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentRSDRPSupportForBill min = 0 max = rsdrp_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentLKDPSupportForBill min = 0 max = lkdp_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentRKDPSupportForBill min = 0 max = rkdp_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentVNSSupportForBill min = 0 max = vns_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentEPSupportForBill min = 0 max = ep_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentNRPRSupportForBill min = 0 max = nrpr_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentNSNPSupportForBill min = 0 max = nsnp_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentIndependentSupportForBill min = 0 max = independent_total_mp }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentPLSRSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = plsr_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentNSPSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = nsp_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentPSRSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = psr_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentRSDRPSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = rsdrp_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentLKDPSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = lkdp_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentRKDPSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = rkdp_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentVNSSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = vns_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentEPSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = ep_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentNRPRSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = nrpr_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentNSNPSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = nsnp_final_senators }
	clamp_variable = { var = CurrentIndependentSenateSupportForBill min = 0 max = independent_final_senators }
	
	
	set_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = 0 }
	set_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = 0 }
	
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentPLSRSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentNSPSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentPSRSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentRSDRPSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentLKDPSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentRKDPSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentVNSSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentEPSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentNRPRSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentNSNPSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSupport = CurrentIndependentSupportForBill }
	round_variable = CurrentOverallSupport
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentPLSRSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentNSPSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentPSRSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentRSDRPSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentLKDPSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentRKDPSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentVNSSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentEPSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentNRPRSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentNSNPSenateSupportForBill }
	add_to_variable = { CurrentOverallSenateSupport = CurrentIndependentSenateSupportForBill }
	round_variable = CurrentOverallSenateSupport 
}
RUS_pass_current_law = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_MERGE_PM_PRESIDENT
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_MERGE_PM_PRESIDENT
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_MERGE_PM_PRESIDENT_accepted
		country_event = {
			id = rusdem.372
			days = 3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_NEP
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_NEP
		set_country_flag = nep_accepted
		country_event = {
			id = rusdem.307
			days = 2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_NATIONALIZATION_TRADE_UNIONS
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_NATIONALIZATION_TRADE_UNIONS
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_NATIONALIZATION_TRADE_UNIONS_accepted
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		SOV_decrease_tomsky = yes
		add_ideas = trade_unions_3
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_IMPEACH_PRESIDENT
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_IMPEACH_PRESIDENT
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_PRESIDENT_WILL_BE_IMPEACHED
		country_event = rusdem.107
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_PSR_SOCIALIZATION_OF_LAND
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_PSR_SOCIALIZATION_OF_LAND
		set_country_flag = soc_land_accepted
		country_event = rusdem.416
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_TU_IMPARTIALITY
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_TU_IMPARTIALITY
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_TU_IMPARTIALITY_accepted
		add_ideas = RUS_trade_unions_impartiality
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SOCIAL_WELFARE
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SOCIAL_WELFARE
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SOCIAL_WELFARE_accepted
		add_ideas = RUS_cheap_housing
		add_ideas = social_security
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 25
		RUS_increase_psr_pop = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_STATE_REGULATION
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_STATE_REGULATION
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_STATE_REGULATION_accepted
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = RUS_industrial_zones
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_industrial_zones
				add_idea = RUS_state_regulation
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_FAIR_LABOUR_ACT
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_FAIR_LABOUR_ACT
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_FAIR_LABOUR_ACT_accepted
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = social_security
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = social_security
				add_idea = RUS_fair_labour
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = RUS_fair_labour
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_PSR_NEW_CONST
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_PSR_NEW_CONST
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_PSR_NEW_CONST_accepted
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.12
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Reassure_Unity_With_NRPR
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = 0.12
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.12
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = "The government will now have more power"
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_INDUSTRIAL_ZONES
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_INDUSTRIAL_ZONES
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_INDUSTRIAL_ZONES_accepted
		add_ideas = RUS_industrial_zones
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_LAW_INDUSTRIAL_ZONES_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS_increase_psr_pop = yes
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { region = 14 }
			increase_state_category_by_one_level = yes
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_LAND_QUOTAS
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_LAND_QUOTAS
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_LAND_QUOTAS_accepted
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = RUS_The_Land_Quotas_Bill }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_LOCAL_PARLIAMENTS
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_LOCAL_PARLIAMENTS
		set_country_flag = loc_parl_accepted
		add_ideas = local_parliaments
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_NATIONAL_AGRARIAN_FUND
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_NATIONAL_AGRARIAN_FUND
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_NATIONAL_AGRARIAN_FUND_accepted
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		destroy_unfinished_land_reform = yes
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 250 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 257 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 254 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 224 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 222 decision = RUS_Mechanize_Agriculture_In_State } #Simbirsk
		add_ideas = RUS_national_agrarian_fund
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SIBERIAN_AUTONOMY
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SIBERIAN_AUTONOMY
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_SIBERIAN_AUTONOMY_accepted
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_siberia = yes
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_siberian_autonomous_republic }  
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_LAW_AGRICULTURAL_COMMITTEE
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_LAW_AGRICULTURAL_COMMITTEE
		set_country_flag = RUS_LAW_AGRICULTURAL_COMMITTEE_accepted
		add_ideas = RUS_agricultral_committee
	}
